           <script>
            $("#min-price").change(function() {
    
    var opt = $(this).find('option:selected');
    
    if(typeof $(opt).attr('data-min-price') !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; typeof $(opt).attr('data-max-price') !== 'undefined') {
      $("#search-price-min").val($(opt).data("min-price"));
      $("#search-price-max").val($(opt).data("max-price"));
    }
  });

    $("#search-properties").focus(function() {
        if($(this).val() == $(this).attr('placeholder')) {
            $(this).val('');
        }
    });

    $("#search-properties").blur(function() {
        if($(this).val() == '') {
            $(this).val($(this).attr("placeholder"));
        }
    });


    $("#rws-responsive-listing-search-369 .search-button").click(function(e) {

        e.preventDefault();

        var frm = $("#rws-responsive-listing-search-369 form.search-form")[0];
        if($("input[name='view']:checked").val() == "map") {
            $(frm).attr({action:'/map/toronto'});
        }
        $(frm).submit();

    });

    $.widget( "custom.catcomplete", $.ui.autocomplete, {
        _renderMenu: function( ul, items ) {
            var self = this,
                currentCategory = "";
            $.each( items, function( index, item ) {
                if ( item.category != currentCategory ) {
                    ul.append( "&lt;li class='ui-autocomplete-category'&gt;" + item.category + "&lt;/li&gt;" );
                    currentCategory = item.category;
                }
                self._renderItemData( ul, item );
            });
            $( ul ).find( "li:odd" ).addClass( "oddMenuItem" );
        }
    });

    $(function() {
        $( "#search-properties" ).catcomplete({
            delay: 0,
            appendTo: "#search-form",
            source: function(req, resp) {

                $.getJSON("/syndicated/locations/auto.php", {
                    l: $("#search-properties").val()
                }, resp);
              },
            minLength: 3
        });

    });
           </script>
           <style>
            .ui-autocomplete {
    max-height: 300px;
    overflow-y: auto;
    /* prevent horizontal scrollbar */
    overflow-x: hidden;
  }
  /* IE 6 doesn't support max-height
   * we use height instead, but this forces the menu to always be this tall
   */
  * html .ui-autocomplete {
    min-height: 100px;
  }
           </style>

         <script>
          (function() {

                var tt = -1;

                var transplode = function(plist) {

                    var pages = $(plist).children("li").detach();
                    var bucket;

                    plist = $(plist).parent().html('');

                    var cols = pages.length &gt; 4 ? 4 : pages.length;
                    var rows = Math.ceil(pages.length / cols);
                    var i = 0;
                    var ind = 0;

                    var remaining = pages.length;
                    var remaining_cols = cols;

                    for(i = 0; i &lt; cols; i++) {

                        bucket = $('&lt;ul /&gt;');
                        bucket = $(bucket).append($(pages).slice(ind, ind + rows));
                        $(plist).append(bucket);
                        remaining -= rows;
                        ind += rows;
                        remaining_cols = remaining_cols - 1;

                        if(remaining &lt; remaining_cols * rows) {
                                rows = Math.ceil( remaining / remaining_cols );
                        }

                     }

                };
 
                var init = function() {

                    $('#rws-responsive-menu-button').sidr({
                        name: 'sidr-main',
                        source: '#rws-navigation'
                    });

                    $("#rws-navigation").on("mouseenter ", "#rws-nav-menu &gt; li", function(e) {
                        if(tt &gt; 0) {
                            clearTimeout(tt);
                        }
                        $("#rws-nav-menu &gt; li").removeClass("hover-menu");
                        var pos = $(this).position();
                        $(".sub-menu", this).css({top:(pos.top + $(this).outerHeight(true)) + "px"});
                        $(this).addClass("hover-menu");
                    });

                    $("#rws-navigation").on("mouseleave", "#rws-nav-menu &gt; li", function(e) {

                        if(tt &gt; 0) {
                            clearTimeout(tt);
                        }
                        tt = setTimeout(function() {
                               $("#rws-nav-menu &gt; li").removeClass("hover-menu");
                                $(this).removeClass("nav-active");
                            }, 500);
                    });

                    $("#rws-nav-menu li ul").each(function() {
                        transplode(this);
                    });

                };

                init();

            })();
         </script>
        </div>
       </div>

          <script>
           $("#tpl_mmenu").on("click", ".tplm_cat &gt; a[href=#]", function(e) {

					e.preventDefault();

					var $subm = $("ul", $(this).parent());

					if($(this).attr("data-collapsing") == "1") {
						$("#tpl_mmenu .tplm_pages_open").not($subm)
						.removeClass("tplm_pages_open")
						.addClass("tplm_pages_closed")
						.css({display:"none"});
						$("#tpl_mmenu .tplm_cat_open").not($(this))
						.removeClass("tplm_cat_open")
						.addClass("tplm_cat_closed");
					}

					if($subm.hasClass("tplm_pages_open")) {
						$subm.addClass("tplm_pages_closed").removeClass("tplm_pages_open").css({display:"none"});
						$(this).removeClass("tplm_cat_open").addClass("tplm_cat_closed");
					} else {
						$subm.addClass("tplm_pages_open").removeClass("tplm_pages_closed").css({display:"block"});
						$(this).removeClass("tplm_cat_closed").addClass("tplm_cat_open");
					}

				});

				$("#tplm_drop")
				.on("mouseenter", ".tplm_cat", function (e) {

					e.preventDefault();

					var $subm = $("ul", $(this));

					$("#tplm_drop .tplm_pages_open").not($subm)
					.removeClass("tplm_pages_open")
					.addClass("tplm_pages_closed")
					.css({display:"none"});

					$("#tplm_drop .tplm_cat_open").not($(".tplm_cat_open",$(this)))
					.removeClass("tplm_cat_open")
					.addClass("tplm_cat_closed");

					$subm.addClass("tplm_pages_open").removeClass("tplm_pages_closed");
					$(".tplm_cat_closed",$(this)).removeClass("tplm_cat_closed").addClass("tplm_cat_open");
				})
				.on("mouseleave", ".tplm_cat", function (e) {

					e.preventDefault();

					var $subm = $("ul", $(this));

					$subm.addClass("tplm_pages_closed").removeClass("tplm_pages_open");
					$(".tplm_cat_open",$(this)).removeClass("tplm_cat_open").addClass("tplm_cat_closed");
				});
          </script>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>

                 <h2 style="text-align: center;">
                  <span style="font-size: 24pt;">
                   <strong>
                    <a href="http://www.sunnybatra.com/Smart-House-Condos" target="_self">
                     <span style="color:#ffffff;">
                      <span style="font-size: 30pt;">
                       Smart House Condos
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </a>
                   </strong>
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <p style="text-align: center;">
                  <span style="font-size:17pt;">
                   <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                    <strong>
                     <a href="#Register">

             <p>
             </p>
             <table align="center" border="1" cellpadding="2" cellspacing="0" height="124" style="width: 944px;" width="903">
              <tbody>
               <tr>
                <td style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 204);">
                 <h3 align="center">
                  <span style="font-size:12pt;">
                   <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                    <span style="color:#ff0000;">
                     <span style="font-size: 14pt;">
                      <strong>
                       Smart House Condos Brings The Best of Micro-living in the Heart of Toronto
                      </strong>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </h3>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     <strong>
                      Smart House Condos, On Queen Street West
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     With the house prices in Downtown Toronto being out of reach of most homebuyers, an increasing number of people who want to be right where the action is are looking for small, affordable units. Smart House being built on Queen Street is designed with just such people in mind. With extremely efficient utilization of every inch of space, the pre-furnished condos of Smart House offer the best of micro-living at the most affordable rates right in the heart of Toronto.
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     <strong>
                      Smart House Building
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     Designed by Architects Alliance, Smart House is a 25-storey boutique building with 241 residential suites that range from studios to 3 bedrooms. The 1st and 2nd floors of the building have 8,000 square feet of retail space and the 3rd and 4th floors have 17,000 square feet of office space. The building has protected views to the east and west as the place is part of the Heritage Conservation District. With super-efficient, highly functional units, a full 50% of which are priced under $300,000, Smart House condos are an investor's dream.
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     <strong>
                      Location of Smart House Condos
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     What is so attractive about Smart House is its incredible location. With a walk score of a perfect 100, which means that technically you never need a car, it is located just a few minutes' walking distance from universities, subway stations, several cafes, restaurants, hotels, banks, hospitals, shops, galleries, theatres, concert halls and stadiums. Everything anyone needs is within walking distance. The building offers an incredible panoramic view of the city of Toronto with the CN Tower on the south and the financial district to the east.
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     Owning a condo in a prime location is what everyone wants, and Smart House Condos will give you just that. The demand for these condos is expected to be very high as close to half a million people work in Downtown Toronto. In addition to that,
                     <strong>
                      53,000+ students
                     </strong>
                     go to the University of Toronto,
                     <strong>
                      39,000+ people
                     </strong>
                     work in the surrounding hospitals and
                     <strong>
                      150,000+ people
                     </strong>
                     walk from College to Queen between Spadina and Yonge every week.
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     <strong>
                      The concept of micro-living
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     The condos incorporate the concept of micro-living in its finest form by utilizing every cubic foot of space to maximize the available living space in the hotel-sized suits (300  500 sq. ft). Examples include sofas with a shelf above it that turns into a bed, a multi-compartment closet with a shelf at the top, pullout cooking board in the kitchen and pantry-style drawers under the bathroom sink. Every single square inch of the suites is utilized to create a comfortable living space, making the suites perfect for students as well as professionals, including the corporate crowds.
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     <strong>
                      Return on Investment (ROI)
                     </strong>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <span style="color:#000000;">
                   <span style="font-size: 12pt;">
                    <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                     Smart House offers the perfect opportunities for those looking to invest in Downtown Toronto. With an average price of $300,000 per unit, the projected return on investment (ROI) from an unfurnished one bedroom suite is 12% and from a furnished one bedroom suite is 14% after tax, mortgage and other payments. This makes the condos incredibly attractive for home owners as well as investors.
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p style="text-align: center;">
                  <span style="font-size:12pt;">
                   <span style="font-family: arial,helvetica,sans-serif;">
                    <span style="background-color:#ffff00;">
                     <strong>
                      <a href="#Register">
                       <span style="color:#0000cd;">
                        Register Below
                       </span>
                      </a>
                     </strong>
                     <span style="color:#000000;">
                      <strong>
                       to get more info &amp; to get Insider's Access &amp; Insiders Platinum Pricing For Smart House Condos
                      </strong>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                </td>
               </tr>
